### [352] [3DGS$^3$: Joint Super Sampling and Frame Interpolation for Real-Time Large-Scale 3DGS Rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11489)
*Yibo Zhao,Fan Gao,Youcheng Cai,Ligang Liu*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出3DGS$^3$，一个基于后渲染的统一框架，通过GASS模块（利用3DGS可微性进行梯度感知超采样）和LTFI模块（轻量级时序帧插值），在低分辨率输出上实现高分辨率和高帧率渲染，兼顾效率与质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在超密集场景和高分辨率下存在计算瓶颈，难以用于延迟敏感应用。现有工作多聚焦于优化渲染管线本身，本文另辟蹊径，从后渲染角度切入。

Method: 提出3DGS$^3$后渲染框架，包含两个核心模块：1) GASS（梯度感知超采样），利用3DGS的连续可微性提取图像梯度，指导GRU网络进行高保真超采样；2) LTFI（轻量级时序帧插值），基于紧凑U-Net骨干网络，融合时序与可微空间线索合成中间帧。

Result: 在公开数据集上，3DGS$^3$在渲染效率和视觉质量上均优于现有方法，且与已有3DGS加速技术兼容。

Conclusion: 3DGS$^3$是一种有效的后渲染方案，能在不修改原始渲染管线的前提下，同时提升分辨率和帧率，具有良好的实用性和扩展性。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) enables high-quality real-time 3D rendering but faces challenges in efficiently scaling to ultra-dense scenes and high-resolution due to computational bottlenecks that limit its use in latency-sensitive applications. Instead of optimizing the splatting pipeline itself, we propose \textbf{3DGS$^3$}, a unified post-rendering framework that jointly performs super sampling and frame interpolation through differentiable processing of low-resolution outputs to achieve both high-resolution and high-frame-rate rendering. Our \textbf{Gradient\- \-Aware Super Sampling (GASS)} module leverages the continuous differentiability of 3DGS to extract image gradients that guide a GRU-based refinement network to enable high-fidelity super sampling. Furthermore, a \textbf{Lightweight Temporal Frame Interpolation (LTFI)} module based on a compact U-Net-like backbone fuses temporal and differentiable spatial cues from consecutive frames to synthesize temporally coherent intermediate frames. Experiments on public datasets demonstrate that 3DGS$^3$ achieves superior rendering efficiency and visual quality when compared with state-of-the-art methods and remains compatible with existing 3DGS acceleration techniques. The code will be publicly released upon acceptance.

</details>


### [353] [ToF ReSTIR: Time-of-Flight Rendering with Spatio-temporal Reservoir Resampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11536)
*Juhyeon Kim,Wojciech Jarosz,Adithya Pediredla*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于时空复用框架的飞行时间(ToF)渲染方法，通过引入路径长度感知的偏移映射(基于牛顿法的几何变换)，显著提升了复杂动态场景中ToF现象的蒙特卡洛渲染效率，实现了交互帧率下的时间门控和瞬态渲染，并验证了在形状重建和导航等下游应用中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ToF渲染方法计算成本高、难以扩展到复杂动态场景，无法满足严格延迟约束下的应用需求。

Method: 借鉴ReSTIR的复用思想，提出路径长度感知的偏移映射，通过牛顿法进行几何变换，强制复用的光路满足物理有效的光程约束。

Result: 在包含光泽/镜面材质和动态运动的复杂场景中显著提升渲染效率，支持交互帧率下的时间门控和瞬态渲染。

Conclusion: 该方法在形状重建和导航等下游应用中展示了实际效果，为交互式ToF模拟提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We present a novel spatio-temporal reuse framework for time-resolved light transport, enabling efficient Monte Carlo rendering of time-of-flight (ToF) phenomena such as time-gated imaging and transient light capture. Existing ToF rendering methods are computationally expensive, scale poorly to complex dynamic scenes, and are therefore unsuitable for applications with strict latency constraints. To address this limitation, we draw inspiration from ReSTIR, a reuse-based technique for steady-state real-time rendering, and adapt its core principles to interactive-rate ToF simulation. However, naively applying existing ReSTIR methods to ToF rendering leads to severe inefficiency, as reused paths frequently violate optical path-length constraints and thus contribute little or no signal. We overcome this challenge by introducing a path reuse formulation that explicitly enforces physically valid optical path lengths. The key idea is path-length-aware shift mapping, a geometric transformation based on Newton's method that adjusts reused light paths to satisfy temporal gating constraints, inspired by specular manifold exploration in steady-state caustics rendering. The resulting framework substantially improves the efficiency of ToF rendering across a wide range of scenarios, including complex scenes with glossy or specular materials and dynamic motion. Our method supports both time-gated and transient rendering at interactive frame rates, enabling simulation under practical latency constraints. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach through two downstream applications, including shape reconstruction and navigation.

</details>


### [354] [STA-FEM: Exact Streaming Assembly for Preplanned Dynamic Tetrahedral Topology Edits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11673)
*Manish Acharya,David Hyde*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出STA-FEM，一种针对动态拓扑四面体网格的流式组装方法，通过在固定超集网格上执行增量更新，避免每次拓扑变化后重建求解器状态，在460k元素规模下实现1.37x-1.61x端到端加速，矩阵更新成本降低数个数量级，并在断裂仿真中实现高达76%的帧时间加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态四面体仿真管线在每次断裂、细化或合并事件后都会重建依赖拓扑的求解器状态，丢弃了每次编辑后仍存续的结构连续性，且将本可局部处理的改动花费全局计算资源。因此，本文旨在解决这一效率瓶颈问题。

Method: STA-FEM采用固定超集网格，预先分配候选单元池，暴露每帧的编辑流。在保持求解器、预条件器、时间步进层不变的前提下，将每帧的组装步骤替换为持久化的增量更新，精确匹配完整重建方法每帧的结果。

Result: 在多达460k元素的三维案例中，端到端加速比达1.37x-1.61x，矩阵更新成本降低数个数量级，且所有测试帧的矩阵精确一致。在真实断裂仿真管线中，帧时间加速最高达76%，且与ground-truth完整重建算法完全等价。

Conclusion: 精确的流式组装方法可成为模拟动态拓扑四面体网格的实用方法，为高效处理频繁拓扑变化的仿真提供了新思路。

Abstract: Dynamic tetrahedral simulation pipelines rebuild topology-dependent solver state after every fracture, refinement, or merge event - discarding structural continuity that survives each edit and spending global work on what are often local changes. We present STA-FEM, a streaming assembly method for simulations with topologically-dynamic tetrahedral meshes operating on a fixed superset mesh: when the candidate element pool is preallocated and the per-frame edit stream is exposed, the surrounding solver, preconditioner, and time-stepping layers stay unchanged while the per-frame assembly step is replaced with persistent incremental updates that match a full-rebuild approach exactly at every frame. Across various three-dimensional examples with up to 460k elements, the method delivers end-to-end speedups of 1.37x to 1.61x over full-rebuild with orders-of-magnitude reductions in matrix update cost, preserving exact matrix parity in all tested frames against a stronger exact local recomputation baseline. We test our algorithm in realistic fracture simulation pipelines and observe up to 76% speedups in fracture frame time with exact equivalence to a ground-truth full-rebuild algorithm. These results establish exact streaming assembly as a potentially practical approach for simulating tetrahedral meshes with dynamic topology.

</details>
